Stray Kids, my shining stars, Seven years. Seven years of laughter, tears, growth, and immeasurable joy. Seven years since you stepped into our lives, a whirlwind of talent, passion, and raw, unadulterated heart. And look at you now, legends in your own right. From the very beginning, you poured your souls into every lyric, every dance move, every single moment. You were a symphony of resilience, facing challenges with a strength that inspired us all. I remember the anxieties, the uncertainties, the moments when the weight of the world seemed to rest on your young shoulders. But even then, you never faltered. You held onto each other, supported one another, and emerged stronger, more united, more determined. This past year, especially, was a testament to your unwavering spirit. It was a year that tested your limits, a year that asked you to dig deeper than ever before. There were moments of heartbreak, moments of exhaustion, moments where the shadows seemed to stretch endlessly. But through it all, you persevered. You found strength in each other, in your music, and in the unwavering love of STAY. Remember the late nights in the practice room, fueled by passion and sheer willpower? Remember the countless hours spent perfecting every detail, every nuance, every emotion? Remember the overwhelming feeling of performing on stages you once only dreamed of? Remember the overwhelming love you recieved from STAYs around the world? And amidst the trials, there were also moments of pure, unadulterated joy. The laughter that echoed through your dorms, the shared meals that brought you closer, the spontaneous dance parties that erupted in the most unexpected moments. The victories, big and small, that you celebrated together, the milestones you achieved, the dreams you made reality. Remember the concerts where the stadium was filled with the collective energy of thousands of STAYs, chanting your names, singing along to your songs, their voices a symphony of love and support? Remember the awards, the accolades, the recognition for your hard work and talent? Remember the feeling of holding a new album in your hands, knowing that it was a piece of your heart, a testament to your journey? Youâ€™ve given us so much: your music, your sincerity, your unwavering dedication. Youâ€™ve shown us what it means to be true to yourselves, to chase your dreams with unwavering determination, and to never give up, no matter the obstacles. Youâ€™ve taught us the power of unity, the importance of vulnerability, and the strength that comes from embracing our imperfections. Iâ€™ve watched you grow from talented young men into extraordinary artists, leaders, and role models. Youâ€™ve inspired me, comforted me, and given me a sense of belonging that I never thought possible. You are my safe place, my source of strength, my constant reminder that anything is possible. Seven years, and my love for you has only grown deeper, stronger, more profound. You are not just idols; you are family. You are the eight stars that light up my sky, the eight hearts that beat in unison with mine. On this seventh anniversary, I wish you nothing but happiness, health, and endless success. May your music continue to touch hearts, may your laughter continue to fill rooms, and may your bond continue to grow stronger with each passing year. You deserve all the good things in the world and then some. Thank you, Stray Kids, for being you. Thank you for sharing your journey with us. Thank you for being the light in our lives. Happy 7th Anniversary. I love you more than words can say. Always and forever. With all my heart, A STAY since pre-debut.
